			<div id='article-section-wrapper'>
	<div id='article-section' role='presentation'>
		<div class='AppleTopic apd-topic dark-mode-enabled book book-content'>
			<div><body dir="ltr" id="mh15189" class="AppleTopic apd-topic dark-mode-enabled" data-istaskopen="true" data-designversion="2" lang="en"><a name="mh15189"></a><figure class="topicIcon"><img src="https://help.apple.com/assets/65E218FE85FC4D5CE50E7794/65E2190393CE9DC994014CA3/en_US/27c443b36b4746b1265c1db0da08868b.png" alt="" height="30" width="30" originalImageName="SharedGlobalArt/AppIconTopic_UsersGroups.png"></figure><h1>Open items automatically when you log in on Mac</h1><p>On your Mac, use Login Items &amp; Extensions settings to choose which items open automatically whenever you log in.</p><div id="mchlpff007b4" class="Task"><h2 aria-controls="aria-mchlpff007b4" class="Name">Add or remove automatic items</h2><div class="TaskBody" role="region" aria-hidden="false" id="aria-mchlpff007b4"><p>You can have apps, documents, folders, or server connections open automatically whenever you log in to your Mac.</p><ol><li><p>On your Mac, choose Apple menu <picture><source media="(not all)" srcset="https://help.apple.com/assets/65E218FE85FC4D5CE50E7794/65E2190393CE9DC994014CA3/en_US/0e2c53fa5a413cc7ff5099226fb50188.png" originalImageName="SharedGlobalArt/IL_AppleLogo_11~dark.png"></source><img src="https://help.apple.com/assets/65E218FE85FC4D5CE50E7794/65E2190393CE9DC994014CA3/en_US/2f77cc85238452e25cb517130188bf99.png" alt="" height="30" width="24" originalImageName="SharedGlobalArt/IL_AppleLogo_11.png"></picture> &gt; System Settings, then click General <img src="https://help.apple.com/assets/65E218FE85FC4D5CE50E7794/65E2190393CE9DC994014CA3/en_US/7c4faef8373d3d73052729c76d485046.png" alt="" height="30" width="30" originalImageName="SharedGlobalArt/AppIconTopic_General.png"> in the sidebar.)</p></li><li><p>Click Login Items &amp; Extensions. (You may need to scroll down.)</p><p><a href="x-help-action://openPrefPane?bundleId=com.apple.LoginItems-Settings.extension" class="URL">Open Login Items &amp; Extensions settings for me</a></p></li><li><p>Do any of the following:</p><ul><li><p><em>Add a login item: </em>Click <img src="https://help.apple.com/assets/65E218FE85FC4D5CE50E7794/65E2190393CE9DC994014CA3/en_US/a2ef32e34a5573d192b10d340a4f46b1.png" alt="the Add button" height="30" width="30" originalImageName="SharedGlobalArt/IL_Plus.png"> below the list of items, select a document, folder, app, server, or other item, then click Add.</p></li><li><p><em>Remove a login item: </em>Select the name of the item you want to prevent from opening automatically, then click <img src="https://help.apple.com/assets/65E218FE85FC4D5CE50E7794/65E2190393CE9DC994014CA3/en_US/e9a8ab65e535ed110ae953650c55ee0c.png" alt="the Remove button" height="30" width="29" originalImageName="SharedGlobalArt/IL_Minus.png"> below the list.</p></li><li><p><em>Allow apps to run in the background: </em>Turn on the app to allow it to perform tasks when the app isn’t open, such as checking for software updates or syncing data.</p></li></ul></li></ol></div></div><div id="mchlp73c3433" class="Task"><h2 aria-controls="aria-mchlp73c3433" class="Name">Temporarily prevent items from opening automatically when you log in</h2><div class="TaskBody" role="region" aria-hidden="false" id="aria-mchlp73c3433"><ul><li><p>If you see the login window, press and hold the Shift key while you click the Log In button, then release the Shift key when the <a href="https://support.apple.com/guide/mac-help/aside/glosc3855c74/15.0/mac/15.0" class="xRef Aside">Dock</a> opens.</p></li><li><p>If you don’t see the login window, restart your Mac, press and hold the Shift key when you see the progress bar in the startup window, then release the Shift key after the desktop appears.</p></li></ul></div></div><div class="LinkUniversal"><strong>See also</strong><a href="https://support.apple.com/guide/mac-help/change-login-items-extensions-settings-mtusr003/15.0/mac/15.0" class="xRef AppleTopic">Change Login Items &amp; Extensions settings on Mac</a><a href="https://support.apple.com/guide/mac-help/change-a-password-or-user-picture-mh35589/15.0/mac/15.0" class="xRef AppleTopic">Change a password or user picture on Mac</a><a href="https://support.apple.com/guide/mac-help/change-users-groups-settings-mtusr001/15.0/mac/15.0" class="xRef AppleTopic">Change Users &amp; Groups settings on Mac</a></div></body></div>
		</div>
	</div>
</div>
